***сверхчеловек.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверхчеловек.html>сверхчеловек</a> (28471)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Übermensch</i>; from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сверх-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sverx-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čelovék</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхчеловек.html>сверхчелове́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sverxčelovék</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхчеловек.html>сверхчелове́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхчеловек.html>сверхчелове́ки</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхчеловек.html>сверхлю́ди</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхчеловек.html>сверхчелове́ков</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхчеловек.html>сверхлюде́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">philosophy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> superman, overman</li>
<li>strong personality whose actions and desires do not obey normal restrictions</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> great man</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">journalistic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nazism" class="extiw" title="w:Nazism">Nazism</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> übermensch, Aryan <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">member of a proposed German master race</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>The irregular plural forms are less common, and unrecognized by some dictionaries.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверхъестественный.html>сверхъесте́ственный</a> (15549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сверх-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sverx-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:естественный.html>есте́ственный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestéstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхъестественный.html>сверхъесте́ственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sverxʺjestéstvennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>supernatural
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхъестественный.html>сверхъесте́ственные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sverxʺjestéstvennyje</b> sposóbnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">supernatural powers</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>extraordinary
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1969</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mikhail_Bulgakov" class="extiw" title="w:Mikhail Bulgakov">Mikhail Bulgakov</a>,  chapter 1, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9C%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B5%D1%80_%D0%B8_%D0%9C%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B3%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B8%D1%82%D0%B0" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Мастер и Маргарита"><a href = vnd.unilang:мастер.html>Ма́стер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маргарит.html>Маргари́та</a></a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбритый.html>вы́бритом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лице́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помещаться.html>помеща́лись</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сверхъестественный.html>сверхъесте́ственных</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:размер.html>разме́ров</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роговой.html>рогово́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оправа.html>опра́ве</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na xorošó výbritom licé jevó pomeščálisʹ <b>sverxʺjestéstvennyx</b> razmérov očkí v čórnoj rogovój opráve.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">On his well-shaved face there were sitting eyeglasses of extraordinary size with black horn frames.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***сверчок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверчок.html>сверчо́к</a> (14198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">свьрчькъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svĭrčĭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svьrčь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверчок.html>сверчо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sverčók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверчок.html>сверчка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверчок.html>сверчки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверчок.html>сверчко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cricket <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">insect</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>grass warbler <i>(Locustella)</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">bird</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***свершаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свершаться.html>сверша́ться</a> (28367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сверша́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sveršátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свершаться.html>сверша́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sveršátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свершиться.html>сверши́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to happen, to occur
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свершаться.html>сверша́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неизбежный.html>неизбе́жное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sveršájetsja</b> neizbéžnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the inevitable is occurring</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come true
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:желание.html>жела́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свершаться.html>сверша́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jejó želánije <b>sveršájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">her wish is coming true</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сверша́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sveršátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***свершиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свершиться.html>сверши́ться</a> (9990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свершить.html>сверши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sveršítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свершиться.html>сверши́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sveršítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свершаться.html>сверша́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to happen, to occur

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свершиться.html>сверши́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неизбежный.html>неизбе́жное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sveršílosʹ</b> neizbéžnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the inevitable has occurred</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come true
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:желание.html>жела́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свершиться.html>сверши́лось</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jejó želánije <b>sveršílosʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">her wish came true</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свершить.html>сверши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sveršítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***свесить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свесить.html>све́сить</a> (12308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>ве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свесить.html>све́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svésitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">све́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let hang, to let down, to lower
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свесить.html>све́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:веревка.html>верёвку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svésitʹ</b> verjóvku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let the rope down; lower the rope</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свесить.html>све́сив</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sidétʹ, <b>svésiv</b> nogi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sit with one's legs dangling</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***свести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a> (3533)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to take <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glaz ne <b>svestí</b> s kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to take one's eyes off someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:могила.html>моги́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svestí</b> kovó-libo v mogílu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring somebody to his grave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svestí</b> s umá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive crazy</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to lead from (one's) mind</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bring together, to throw together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>концы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конца́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svestí</b> koncý s koncámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make both ends meet</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to bring together ends with ends</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жбу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svestí</b> drúžbu s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make friends with someone</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to bring together friendship with someone</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reduce <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to bring <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svestí</b> sčóty s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to settle a score with someone, to square accounts with someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svestí</b> razgovór na štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead the conversation to something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>нулю́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svestí</b> na net, <b>svestí</b> k nuljú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring to nothing, to reduce to zero, to cancel, to invalidate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svestí</b> k šútke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn into a joke</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to remove</li>
<li>to trace <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a picture</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***свет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a> (213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">свѣтъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">světŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*světъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light; world</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svet</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>light
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неоновый.html>нео́новый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neónovyj <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">neon light</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjáxkij <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">soft light</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дневной.html>дневно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dnevnój <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">daylight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:солнечный.html>со́лнечный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sólnečnyj <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sunshine, sunlight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яркий.html>я́ркий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">járkij <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">bright light</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тусклый.html>ту́склый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">túsklyj <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">dim light</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучок.html>пучо́к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pučók <b>svéta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">beam of light</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скорость.html>ско́рость</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skórostʹ <b>svéta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">speed of light</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pri <b>svéte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by the light of</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тушить.html>туши́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tušítʹ <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">turn off the light</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тушь.html>туши́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:бросать.html>броса́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:граната.html>грана́ту</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tuší <b>svet</b>, brosáj granátu!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><span class="use-with-mention">(said when something very unusual happens)</span></span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">turn out the light and toss a grenade!</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>day</li>
<li>radiance</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lights, lighting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повсюду.html>повсю́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Povsjúdu gorél <b>svet</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The lights were on everywhere.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> power, electricity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Opjátʹ net <b>svéta</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There’s no power again!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">свѣтъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">světŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*světъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light; world</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svet</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>world, earth, universe:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́сти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">části <b>svéta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">parts of the world</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вокруг.html>вокру́г</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vokrúg <b>svéta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">round the world</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>коне́ц</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">konéc <b>svéta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">doomsday, the end of the world, Apocalypse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vesʹ <b>svet</b>, célyj <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the whole world</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объездить.html>объе́здил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> краси́вей <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja obʺjézdil célyj <b>svet</b>, no tebjá krasívej net</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I traveled all over the whole world but didn’t find a woman more beautiful than you</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скитаться.html>скита́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> бе́лу <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́ту</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skitátʹsja po bélu <b>svétu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock about the world</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́те</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni za što na <b>svéte</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not for the world!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bólʹše vsevó na <b>svéte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">above all, above everything</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люблю́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́те</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja ljubljú tebjá bólʹše vsevó na <b>svéte</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I love you more than anything</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клин.html>кли́ном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сойтись.html>сошёлся</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svet</b> klínom ne sošólsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the world is large enough, there are other fish in the sea</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругать.html>руга́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rugátʹ na čóm <b>svet</b> stoít</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to swear like nothing on earth, curse like hell, curse a blue streak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tot <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the next world</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отправиться.html>отпра́виться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otprávitʹsja na tot <b>svet</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to go to the next world<i>, </i>to die</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pojavítʹsja na <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be born, to come into the world</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвести.html>произвести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">proizvestí na <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give birth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпустить.html>вы́пустить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výpustitʹ v <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to publish, to bring out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увидеть.html>уви́деть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">uvídetʹ <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be born, to be published</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bélyj <b>svet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this world, the world</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>society, people, aristocracy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сший</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщества</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výsšij <b>svet</b> (óbščestva)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">upper crust, high society</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светать.html>света́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

***светило.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>светило</a> (4847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светить.html>свети́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>свети́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svetílo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>свети́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>свети́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>свети́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heavenly body, celestial body, lamp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дневной.html>дневно́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>свети́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dnevnóje <b>svetílo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the star of day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночной.html>ночны́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>свети́ла</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nočnýje <b>svetíla</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the moon and the stars; the lamps of night</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>luminary, notability
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>свети́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наука.html>нау́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svetílo</b> naúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a luminary [leading light] in science</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светило.html>свети́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svetílo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">neuter singular past indicative imperfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светить.html>свети́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светить.html>свети́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светиться.html>свети́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svetítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to shine, to glow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to attract (unwanted) attention</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светить.html>свети́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***светлеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:светлеть.html>светле́ть</a> (12323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светлый.html>све́тлый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svétlyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светлеть.html>светле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svetlétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посветлеть.html>посветле́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просветлеть.html>просветле́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lighten, to become lighter</li>
<li>to be visible <i>(of a light-coloured object)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a> что́-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:светлеть.html>светле́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vdalí štó-to <b>svetlélo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there was [one could see / detect] a light-coloured spot in the distance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">засветле́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zasvetlétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посветлеть.html>посветле́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">posvetlétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просветлеть.html>просветле́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prosvetlétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***светлый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:светлый.html>све́тлый</a> (1194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*světьlъ</i>; synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светлый.html>све́тлый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svétlyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)светле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:светлеть.html>светле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>light (having light), bright</li>
<li>jolly</li></ol>

***светофор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:светофор.html>светофо́р</a> (8862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φορός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phorós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">carrying</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светофор.html>светофо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svetofór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светофор.html>светофо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светофор.html>светофо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светофор.html>светофо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>traffic light</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светоч.html>све́точ</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svétoč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светоч.html>све́точа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светоч.html>све́точи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светоч.html>све́точей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">lofty</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lamp, luminary, light
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:светоч.html>све́точ</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:истина.html>и́стины</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svétoč</b> ístiny</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the light of truth</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:светоч.html>све́точ</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ды</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:познание.html>позна́ния</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svétoč</b> svobódy (poznánija)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the lamp/torch of freedom (learning)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
